--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

MainWindow.xaml.cs

using GraphX.Common.Enums;
using GraphX.Controls;
using GraphX.Logic.Models;
using Microsoft.Win32;
using NKM1.DTO;
using NKM1.Impulse;
using NKM1.Models;
using NKM1.Service;
using NKM1.Visual;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.ComponentModel;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Windows;
using System.Windows.Controls;
using System.Windows.Media;

namespace NKM1
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Interaction logic for MainWindow.xaml
    /// Здесь добавлены: коллекция ImpulseRows и перенос управления списком импульсов.
    /// </summary>
    public partial class MainWindow : Window
    {
        private DataGraphLogicCore? graphLogic;
        private NKM? graph;

        // Новое: список строк импульсов, управляемый MainWindow.
        // Эту коллекцию мы передаём в ImpulseWindow (в конструктор).
        private List<VertexImpulseRow> ImpulseRows = new List<VertexImpulseRow>();

        public MainWindow()
        {
            InitializeComponent();

            // Пример: создаём случайный граф для демонстрации
            graph = NKM.CreateRandomDirectedGraph(5, 10, 123);
            graphLogic = new DataGraphLogicCore(graph);
            graphArea.LogicCore = graphLogic;
            ZoomControl.SetViewFinderVisibility(ZoomCtrl, Visibility.Visible);
            graphArea.SetupSettings();

            RefreshLists();
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Обновляет списки вершин и рёбер в элементах управления (ListBox’ы),
        /// а также синхронизирует ImpulseRows в соответствии с текущим графом.
        /// </summary>
        private void RefreshLists()
        {
            // Обновляем список вершин
            LstVertices.ItemsSource = null;
            LstVertices.ItemsSource = graph?.Vertices.Select(v => v.Name).OrderBy(v => v).ToList();

            // Обновляем список рёбер
            LstEdges.ItemsSource = null;
            LstEdges.ItemsSource = graph?.Edges
                .Select(e => $"{e.Source?.Name}-{e.Target?.Name} : {e.Weight}")
                .OrderBy(e => e)
                .ToList();

            // Перерисовываем визуализацию графа
            UpdateGraphAreaFromModel();

            // === Синхронизация ImpulseRows с текущими вершинами графа ===
            // Сохраним существующие значения импульсов по имени вершины
            var existingByName = ImpulseRows.ToDictionary(r => r.Vertex?.ID ?? -1, r => r);

            var newRows = new List<VertexImpulseRow>();
            if (graph != null)
            {
                foreach (var v in graph.Vertices)
                {
                    // Если уже есть строка для данной вершины (по ID), сохраним её значения
                    if (existingByName.TryGetValue(v.ID, out var existRow))
                    {
                        existRow.Vertex = v;
                        existRow.Name = v.Name;
                        newRows.Add(existRow);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        // новая строка — по умолчанию импульс 0
                        newRows.Add(new VertexImpulseRow
                        {
                            Vertex = v,
                            Name = v.Name,
                            Impulse = "0.0",
                            IsVisible = false
                        });
                    }
                }
            }

            ImpulseRows = newRows;

            // Привязываем ItemsControl в MainWindow к ImpulseRows
            ImpulsesList.ItemsSource = null;
            ImpulsesList.ItemsSource = ImpulseRows;

            // --- подписываемся на изменение IsVisible ---
            foreach (var row in ImpulseRows)
            {
                row.PropertyChanged -= VertexRow_PropertyChanged;
                row.PropertyChanged += VertexRow_PropertyChanged;
            }
        }

        private void VertexRow_PropertyChanged(object? sender, PropertyChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.PropertyName == nameof(VertexImpulseRow.IsVisible))
            {
                var row = sender as VertexImpulseRow;
                if (row?.Vertex == null || graphArea == null) return;

                // найти визуальный контрол вершины в GraphX
                if (graphArea.VertexList.TryGetValue(row.Vertex, out var vertexControl))
                {
                    if (row.IsVisible)
                    {
                        vertexControl.Background = Brushes.LightYellow; // вершина подсвечивается красным
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        vertexControl.Background = Brushes.White; // стандартный цвет 
                    }
                }
            }
        }


        /// <summary>
        /// Строит визуальный граф в GraphArea на основании текущей модели (graph).
        /// (исходная логика перенесена из проекта)
        /// </summary>
        private void UpdateGraphAreaFromModel()
        {
            if (graphArea == null || graphLogic == null || graph == null) return;

            // Генерируем визуальные контролы (VertexControl / EdgeControl)
            try
            {
                graphArea.GenerateGraph(true, true);
            }
            catch
            {
                try { graphArea.GenerateGraph(true); } catch { graphArea.RelayoutGraph(); }
            }

            
            try
            {
                // Устанавливаем подписи рёбер (веса)
                foreach (var kv in graphArea.EdgesList)
                {
                    var edgeControl = kv.Value;
                    if (edgeControl == null) continue;
                    var dataEdge = edgeControl.Edge as Link;
                    if (dataEdge is not null)
                    {
                        // Ищем элемент TextBlock с именем "PART_EdgeLabel" внутри EdgeControl
                        var label = FindVisualChildByName(edgeControl, "PART_EdgeLabel") as TextBlock;
                        if (label is not null) label.Text = dataEdge.Weight.ToString();
                            edgeControl.ToolTip = dataEdge.Weight.ToString();
                        if (dataEdge.Weight >= 0)
                        {
                            if (label is not null)
                            {
                                label.Background = Brushes.Green;
                                label.Foreground = Brushes.Green;
                            }
                            edgeControl.Foreground = Brushes.Green;
                            edgeControl.Background = Brushes.Green;
                            edgeControl.DashStyle = EdgeDashStyle.Solid;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            if (label is not null)
                            {
                                label.Background = Brushes.Red;
                                label.Foreground = Brushes.Red;
                            }

                            edgeControl.Foreground = Brushes.Red;
                            edgeControl.Background = Brushes.Red;
                            edgeControl.DashStyle = EdgeDashStyle.Dash;
                        }
                    }
                }

                foreach (var kv in graphArea.VertexList)
                {
                    var vertexControl = kv.Value;
                    if (vertexControl == null) continue;
                    var dataVertex = vertexControl.Vertex as Factor;
                    if (dataVertex != null)
                    {
                        if(ImpulseRows.Any(row => row.Vertex.ID == dataVertex.ID && row.IsVisible))
                            vertexControl.Background = Brushes.LightYellow; // вершина подсвечивается красным
                        else
                            vertexControl.Background = Brushes.White; // стандартный цвет
                    }
                }
            }
            catch { /* не критично */ }
        }

    /// <summary>
    /// Рекурсивный поиск визуального элемента по имени в дереве WPF.
    /// Используется для поиска текстовых меток рёбер.
    /// </summary>
        private FrameworkElement FindVisualChildByName(DependencyObject parent, string name)
        {
            if (parent == null) return null;
            for (int i = 0; i < VisualTreeHelper.GetChildrenCount(parent); i++)
            {
                var child = VisualTreeHelper.GetChild(parent, i);
            if (child is FrameworkElement fe && fe.Name == name)
                return fe;
                var result = FindVisualChildByName(child, name);
                if (result != null) return result;
            }
            return null;
        }

        // --- Обработчики кнопок (оставлены исходные, только BtnImpulse изменён) ---
        private void BtnAddVertex_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var addWindow = new AddVertexWindow(graph) { Owner = this };
            if (addWindow.ShowDialog() == true)
            {
                if (graph.AddVertex(new Factor(addWindow.Name)))
                {
                    RefreshLists();
                    MessageBox.Show($"Добавлен новый фактор '{addWindow.Name}'", "Успешно", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Information);
                }
                else
                {
                    MessageBox.Show("Не удалось добавить фактор", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Error);
                }
            }
        }

        private void BtnRemoveVertex_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (LstVertices.SelectedItem == null) return;
            var id = LstVertices.SelectedItem.ToString();
            graph.RemoveVertex(id);
            RefreshLists();
        }

        private void BtnAddEdge_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var addEdgeWindow = new AddEdgeWindow(graph) { Owner = this };
            if (addEdgeWindow.ShowDialog() == true)
            {
                if (graph.AddEdge(addEdgeWindow.Source, addEdgeWindow.Target, addEdgeWindow.Weight))
                {
                    RefreshLists();
                    MessageBox.Show($"Добавлена новая связь '{addEdgeWindow.Source.Name}' -> '{addEdgeWindow.Target.Name}' с оценкой {addEdgeWindow.Weight}", "Успешно", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Information);
                }
                else
                {
                    MessageBox.Show($"Не удалось добавить связь '{addEdgeWindow.Source.Name}' -> '{addEdgeWindow.Target.Name}'", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Error);
                }
            }
        }

        private void BtnRemoveEdge_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (LstEdges.SelectedItem == null) return;
            var text = LstEdges.SelectedItem.ToString();
            var dash = text.IndexOf('-');
            var colon = text.IndexOf(':');
            var source = text.Substring(0, dash).Trim();
            var target = text.Substring(dash + 1, colon - dash - 1).Trim();
            graph.RemoveEdge(source, target);
            RefreshLists();
        }

        private void BtnSetVertexName_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (LstVertices.SelectedItem == null) { MessageBox.Show("Выберите вершину"); return; }
            var oldName = LstVertices.SelectedItem?.ToString();
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(oldName)) { MessageBox.Show("Выберите вершину"); return; }
            var renameVertexWindow = new RenameVertexWindow(graph, graph.Vertices.First(v => v.Name.Equals(LstVertices.SelectedItem.ToString(), StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))) { Owner = this };
            if (renameVertexWindow.ShowDialog() == true)
            {
                graph.RenameVertex(oldName, renameVertexWindow.NewName);
                RefreshLists();
            }
        }

        private void BtnSetWeight_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (LstEdges.SelectedItem is null) { MessageBox.Show("Выберите связь"); return; }
            var text = LstEdges.SelectedItem.ToString();
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(text)) { MessageBox.Show("Выберите связь"); return; }
            var dash = text.IndexOf('-');
            var colon = text.IndexOf(':');
            var source = text.Substring(0, dash).Trim();
            var target = text.Substring(dash + 1, colon - dash - 1).Trim();
            var link = graph.Edges.FirstOrDefault(e => e.Target.Name.Equals(target) && e.Source.Name.Equals(source));
            if (link is null) { MessageBox.Show("Выберите связь"); return; }
            var editEdgeWindow = new EditEdgeWindow(graph, link) { Owner = this };
            if (editEdgeWindow.ShowDialog() == true)
            {
                if (graph.RemoveEdge(link) && graph.AddEdge(editEdgeWindow.Source, editEdgeWindow.Target, editEdgeWindow.Weight))
                {
                    RefreshLists();
                    MessageBox.Show($"Изменена связь '{link.Source.Name}' -> '{link.Target.Name}' с оценкой {link.Weight} \n на {editEdgeWindow.Source.Name}' -> '{editEdgeWindow.Target.Name}' с оценкой {editEdgeWindow.Weight}", "Успешно", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Information);
                }
            }
        }

        private void BtnLayout_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            try { graphArea?.RelayoutGraph(); } catch (Exception ex) { MessageBox.Show("Layout failed: " + ex.Message); }
        }

        private void BtnCycle_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            new StructureAnalizys(graph).ShowDialog();
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Открываем окно импульсов — передаём ему управляемый MainWindow список ImpulseRows
        /// (и граф для выполнения симуляции).
        /// </summary>
        private void BtnImpulse_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var wnd = new NKM1.Impulse.ImpulseWindow(ImpulseRows, graph);
            wnd.Owner = this;
            wnd.ShowDialog();
        }

        private void BtnSave_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var dlg = new SaveFileDialog { Filter = "Graph files (*.graph)|*.graph", DefaultExt = ".graph" };
            if (dlg.ShowDialog() == true) GraphFileService.Save(graph, graphArea, dlg.FileName);
        }

        private void BtnLoad_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var dlg = new OpenFileDialog { Filter = "Graph files (*.graph)|*.graph", DefaultExt = ".graph" };
            if (dlg.ShowDialog() == true) { GraphFileService.Load(graph, graphArea, dlg.FileName); RefreshLists(); }
        }
    }
}

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

EdgeDto.cs

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Text.Json.Serialization;
using System.Threading.Tasks;

namespace NKM1.DTO
{

    public class EdgeDto
    {
        [JsonPropertyName("vertex1")] public int Vertex1 { get; set; }
        [JsonPropertyName("vertex2")] public int Vertex2 { get; set; }
        // weight в файле — строка, поэтому сохраняем как string
        [JsonPropertyName("weight")] public string Weight { get; set; } = "1.0";
        [JsonPropertyName("isDirected")] public bool IsDirected { get; set; } = true;
        [JsonPropertyName("controlStep")] public int ControlStep { get; set; } = 0;
        [JsonPropertyName("fontSize")] public double FontSize { get; set; } = 18;
        [JsonPropertyName("lineWidth")] public double LineWidth { get; set; } = 2;
        [JsonPropertyName("background")] public string Background { get; set; } = "#000000";
        [JsonPropertyName("color")] public string Color { get; set; } = "#000000";
    }
}

GraphFileDto.cs

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using System.IO;
using System.Text.Json;
using System.Text.Json.Serialization;
using Microsoft.Win32; // OpenFileDialog / SaveFileDialog


namespace NKM1.DTO
{
    public class GraphFileDto
    {
        [JsonPropertyName("x0")] public double X0 { get; set; }
        [JsonPropertyName("y0")] public double Y0 { get; set; }
        [JsonPropertyName("vertices")] public List<VertexDto> Vertices { get; set; } = new List<VertexDto>();
        [JsonPropertyName("edges")] public List<EdgeDto> Edges { get; set; } = new List<EdgeDto>();
        [JsonPropertyName("texts")] public List<object> Texts { get; set; } = new List<object>();
    }
}

VertexDto.cs

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Text.Json.Serialization;
using System.Threading.Tasks;

namespace NKM1.DTO
{
    public class VertexDto
    {
        [JsonPropertyName("x")] public double X { get; set; }
        [JsonPropertyName("y")] public double Y { get; set; }
        [JsonPropertyName("name")] public string Name { get; set; } = "";
        [JsonPropertyName("radius")] public double Radius { get; set; } = 20;
        [JsonPropertyName("background")] public string Background { get; set; } = "#ffffff";
        [JsonPropertyName("fontSize")] public double FontSize { get; set; } = 18;
        [JsonPropertyName("color")] public string Color { get; set; } = "#000000";
        [JsonPropertyName("border")] public string Border { get; set; } = "#000000";
    }
}

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ImpulseWindow.xaml.cs

using Microsoft.Win32;
using NKM1;
using NKM1.Models;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Windows;
using System.Windows.Controls;
using System.Windows.Input;
using System.Windows.Media;
using System.Windows.Shapes;

namespace NKM1.Impulse
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Логика окна импульсов.
    /// </summary>
    public partial class ImpulseWindow : Window
    {
        private readonly NKM _graph;
        private readonly List<VertexImpulseRow> _rows;
        private SimulationResult _lastResult;
        private readonly Brush[] _palette = new Brush[]
        {
            Brushes.Blue, Brushes.Red, Brushes.Green, Brushes.Orange, Brushes.Purple,
            Brushes.Brown, Brushes.Magenta, Brushes.Cyan, Brushes.LimeGreen, Brushes.DarkGoldenrod
        };

        public ImpulseWindow(List<VertexImpulseRow> rows, NKM graph)
        {
            InitializeComponent();

            _rows = rows ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(rows));
            _graph = graph ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(graph));
        }

        private void BtnRun_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (!int.TryParse(TxtSteps.Text.Trim(), out var steps) || steps < 0)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Введите корректное неотрицательное число шагов.");
                return;
            }

            var P0 = new Dictionary<Factor, double>();
            var errors = new StringBuilder();
            foreach (var r in _rows)
            {
                var s = (r?.Impulse ?? "").Trim();
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(s) || s == "0" || s == "0.0" || s == "0,0") continue;
                if (TryParseDoubleFlexible(s, out var val))
                {
                    P0[r.Vertex] = val;
                }
                else
                {
                    errors.AppendLine($"Неверный импульс у вершины {r.Name}: \"{r.Impulse}\"");
                }
            }

            if (errors.Length > 0)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Ошибки ввода:\n" + errors.ToString(), "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Warning);
                return;
            }

            _lastResult = ImpulseSimulator.Simulate(_graph, P0, steps);
            DrawResult(_lastResult);
        }

        private void DrawResult(SimulationResult res)
        {
            PlotCanvas.Children.Clear();
            if (res == null || res.ValuesByStep.Count == 0) return;
            int stepsCount = res.ValuesByStep.Count;
            int nAll = res.VertexNames.Count;
            if (nAll == 0) return;

            // transpose data to per-vertex series (full)
            var fullSeries = new List<double[]>();
            for (int i = 0; i < nAll; i++)
            {
                var arr = new double[stepsCount];
                for (int t = 0; t < stepsCount; t++) arr[t] = res.ValuesByStep[t][i];
                fullSeries.Add(arr);
            }

            // подготовим список видимых рядов по порядку строк _rows
            var visiblePairs = new List<(VertexImpulseRow row, int indexInResult)>();
            var nameToIndex = new Dictionary<string, int>(StringComparer.Ordinal);
            for (int i = 0; i < res.VertexNames.Count; i++) nameToIndex[res.VertexNames[i]] = i;

            foreach (var row in _rows)
            {
                if (!row.IsVisible) continue;
                if (row == null) continue;
                if (!nameToIndex.TryGetValue(row.Name, out var idx)) continue;
                visiblePairs.Add((row, idx));
            }

            double dataMin = fullSeries.SelectMany(a => a).Min();
            double dataMax = fullSeries.SelectMany(a => a).Max();
            if (dataMin == dataMax) { dataMin -= 0.5; dataMax += 0.5; }

            double leftMargin = 70;
            double rightMargin = 30;
            double bottomMargin = 70; 
            double topMargin = 20;
            double wPerStep = Math.Max(24, 40.0);
            double canvasWidth = leftMargin + wPerStep * Math.Max(1, stepsCount - 1) + rightMargin;
            double canvasHeight = Math.Max(300, Math.Min(1200, 450));
            PlotCanvas.Width = canvasWidth;
            PlotCanvas.Height = canvasHeight;
            double plotLeft = leftMargin;
            double plotRight = canvasWidth - rightMargin;
            double plotTop = topMargin;
            double plotBottom = canvasHeight - bottomMargin;
            double ymin = dataMin;
            double ymax = dataMax;

            Func<double, double> valueToY = (val) =>
            {
                double norm = (val - ymin) / (ymax - ymin);
                if (double.IsNaN(norm) || double.IsInfinity(norm)) norm = 0.0;
                return plotBottom - norm * (plotBottom - plotTop);
            };

            // vertical & horizontal axes
            var (tickStart, tickStep, tickCount) = CalculateNiceTicks(ymin, ymax, 6);

            var vAxis = new Line { X1 = plotLeft, Y1 = plotTop, X2 = plotLeft, Y2 = plotBottom, Stroke = Brushes.Black, StrokeThickness = 1.2 };
            PlotCanvas.Children.Add(vAxis);
            var hAxis = new Line { X1 = plotLeft, Y1 = plotBottom, X2 = plotRight, Y2 = plotBottom, Stroke = Brushes.Black, StrokeThickness = 1.0 };
            PlotCanvas.Children.Add(hAxis);

            for (int k = 0; k < tickCount; k++)
            {
                double val = tickStart + k * tickStep;
                double y = valueToY(val);
                var tick = new Line { X1 = plotLeft - 6, Y1 = y, X2 = plotLeft, Y2 = y, Stroke = Brushes.Black, StrokeThickness = 1 };
                PlotCanvas.Children.Add(tick);
                string labelText = FormatNiceNumber(val, tickStep);
                var lbl = new TextBlock { Text = labelText, FontSize = 11 };
                Canvas.SetLeft(lbl, plotLeft - 10 - MeasureTextWidth(labelText, lbl.FontSize));
                Canvas.SetTop(lbl, y - 10);
                PlotCanvas.Children.Add(lbl);
                var grid = new Line { X1 = plotLeft, Y1 = y, X2 = plotRight, Y2 = y, Stroke = Brushes.LightGray, StrokeThickness = 0.6, StrokeDashArray = new DoubleCollection() { 2, 3 } };
                PlotCanvas.Children.Add(grid);
            }

            // draw visible series
            var nameToPolyline = new Dictionary<string, Polyline>(StringComparer.Ordinal);
            for (int i = 0; i < visiblePairs.Count; i++)
            {
                var pair = visiblePairs[i];
                var arr = fullSeries[pair.indexInResult];
                var poly = new Polyline { StrokeThickness = 1.6, Stroke = _palette[i % _palette.Length], SnapsToDevicePixels = true };
                for (int t = 0; t < stepsCount; t++)
                {
                    double x = plotLeft + t * wPerStep;
                    double y = valueToY(arr[t]);
                    poly.Points.Add(new Point(x, y));
                }
                PlotCanvas.Children.Add(poly);
                nameToPolyline[pair.row.Name] = poly;
            }

            // легенда / подписи справа (кликабельно)
            for (int i = 0; i < visiblePairs.Count; i++)
            {
                var pair = visiblePairs[i];
                var name = pair.row.Name;
                var poly = nameToPolyline.ContainsKey(name) ? nameToPolyline[name] : null;
                var txt = new TextBlock { Text = name, Foreground = _palette[i % _palette.Length], FontSize = 12, Cursor = Cursors.Hand };
                Canvas.SetLeft(txt, plotRight + 6);
                Canvas.SetTop(txt, 8 + i * 18);
                txt.MouseLeftButtonDown += (s, e) =>
                {
                    if (poly != null)
                    {
                        var now = poly.Visibility == Visibility.Visible ? Visibility.Collapsed : Visibility.Visible;
                        poly.Visibility = now;
                        var r = _rows.FirstOrDefault(rr => rr.Name == name);
                        if (r != null) r.IsVisible = (now == Visibility.Visible);
                    }
                };
                PlotCanvas.Children.Add(txt);
            }

            // X axis labels
            for (int t = 0; t < stepsCount; t++)
            {
                double x = plotLeft + t * wPerStep;
                var tick = new Line { X1 = x, Y1 = plotBottom, X2 = x, Y2 = plotBottom + 6, Stroke = Brushes.Black, StrokeThickness = 0.8 };
                PlotCanvas.Children.Add(tick);
                var lbl = new TextBlock { Text = t.ToString(System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture), FontSize = 10 };
                Canvas.SetLeft(lbl, x - 6);
                Canvas.SetTop(lbl, plotBottom + 8);
                PlotCanvas.Children.Add(lbl);
            }

            // локальные вспомогательные функции
            static (double start, double step, int count) CalculateNiceTicks(double min, double max, int maxTicks)
            {
                if (max <= min) return (min, 1.0, 2);
                double range = NiceNum(max - min, false);
                double step = NiceNum(range / (maxTicks - 1), true);
                double start = Math.Floor(min / step) * step;
                double end = Math.Ceiling(max / step) * step;
                int count = (int)Math.Round((end - start) / step) + 1;
                return (start, step, count);
            }

            static double NiceNum(double x, bool round)
            {
                double exp = Math.Floor(Math.Log10(x));
                double f = x / Math.Pow(10, exp);
                double nf;
                if (round)
                {
                    if (f < 1.5) nf = 1;
                    else if (f < 3) nf = 2;
                    else if (f < 7) nf = 5;
                    else nf = 10;
                }
                else
                {
                    if (f <= 1) nf = 1;
                    else if (f <= 2) nf = 2;
                    else if (f <= 5) nf = 5;
                    else nf = 10;
                }
                return nf * Math.Pow(10, exp);
            }

            static string FormatNiceNumber(double value, double tickStep)
            {
                int decimals = 0;
                if (tickStep < 1)
                {
                    double tmp = tickStep;
                    while (Math.Abs(Math.Round(tmp) - tmp) > 1e-12 && decimals < 10)
                    {
                        tmp *= 10; decimals++;
                    }
                }
                decimals = Math.Min(decimals, 6);
                return value.ToString("F" + decimals, System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
            }

            double MeasureTextWidth(string text, double fontSize) => text.Length * (fontSize * 0.56);
        }

        private void BtnExportCsv_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (_lastResult == null)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Нечего экспортировать — сначала выполните моделирование.");
                return;
            }

            var sb = new StringBuilder();
            sb.Append("step");
            foreach (var name in _lastResult.VertexNames) sb.Append($";{EscapeCsv(name)}");
            sb.AppendLine();
            for (int t = 0; t < _lastResult.ValuesByStep.Count; t++)
            {
                sb.Append(t);
                var row = _lastResult.ValuesByStep[t];
                for (int i = 0; i < row.Length; i++)
                {
                    sb.Append(";");
                    sb.Append(row[i].ToString(System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture));
                }
                sb.AppendLine();
            }

            var dlg = new Microsoft.Win32.SaveFileDialog { Filter = "CSV|*.csv", FileName = "impulse_result.csv" };
            if (dlg.ShowDialog() == true)
            {
                System.IO.File.WriteAllText(dlg.FileName, sb.ToString(), Encoding.UTF8);
                MessageBox.Show("Сохранено: " + dlg.FileName);
            }
        }

        private string EscapeCsv(string s) => s?.Replace("\"", "\"\"") ?? "";

        private bool TryParseDoubleFlexible(string s, out double value)
        {
            value = 0.0;
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s)) return false;
            if (double.TryParse(s, System.Globalization.NumberStyles.Float | System.Globalization.NumberStyles.AllowThousands, System.Globalization.CultureInfo.CurrentCulture, out value)) return true;
            var alt = s.Replace(',', '.');
            if (double.TryParse(alt, System.Globalization.NumberStyles.Float | System.Globalization.NumberStyles.AllowThousands, System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out value)) return true;
            var trimmed = s.Replace(" ", "");
            if (double.TryParse(trimmed, System.Globalization.NumberStyles.Float | System.Globalization.NumberStyles.AllowThousands, System.Globalization.CultureInfo.CurrentCulture, out value)) return true;
            return false;
        }
    }
}

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CycleEnumerator.cs

using NKM1.Models;
using QuickGraph;

namespace NKM1;

/// <summary>
/// Поиск всех уникальных циклов в графе НКМ и определение их знака.
/// </summary>
public static class CycleDetection
{
    public static List<CycleInfo> FindAllSimpleCycles(
        IBidirectionalGraph<Factor, Link> graph)
    {
        var result = new List<CycleInfo>();
        var visited = new HashSet<Factor>();
        var stack = new Stack<Factor>();
        var currentPath = new HashSet<Factor>();
        var uniqueCycles = new HashSet<string>();

        foreach (var vertex in graph.Vertices)
        {
            DFS(graph, vertex, vertex, visited, stack, currentPath, result, uniqueCycles);
            visited.Add(vertex);
        }

        return result;
    }

    private static void DFS(
        IBidirectionalGraph<Factor, Link> graph,
        Factor startFactor,
        Factor currentFactor,
        HashSet<Factor> visited,
        Stack<Factor> stack,
        HashSet<Factor> currentPath,
        List<CycleInfo> result,
        HashSet<string> uniqueCycles)
    {
        stack.Push(currentFactor);
        currentPath.Add(currentFactor);

        foreach (var edge in graph.OutEdges(currentFactor))
        {
            var next = edge.Target;

            if (next.Equals(startFactor))
            {
                var cycle = stack.Reverse().ToList();
                var key = NormalizeCycle(cycle);

                if (uniqueCycles.Add(key))
                {
                    // вычисляем знак цикла
                    int negativeEdges = CountNegativeEdges(graph, cycle);
                    bool isPositive = negativeEdges % 2 == 0;

                    result.Add(new CycleInfo
                    {
                        Vertices = cycle,
                        IsPositive = isPositive,
                        NegativeEdgeCount = negativeEdges
                    });
                }

                continue;
            }

            if (!visited.Contains(next) && !currentPath.Contains(next))
            {
                DFS(graph, startFactor, next, visited, stack, currentPath, result, uniqueCycles);
            }
        }

        stack.Pop();
        currentPath.Remove(currentFactor);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Подсчёт количества отрицательных рёбер в цикле.
    /// </summary>
    private static int CountNegativeEdges(IBidirectionalGraph<Factor, Link> graph, List<Factor> cycle)
    {
        int count = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < cycle.Count; i++)
        {
            var source = cycle[i];
            var target = cycle[(i + 1) % cycle.Count];

            var edge = graph.Edges.FirstOrDefault(e => e.Source == source && e.Target == target);
            if (edge != null && edge.Weight < 0)
                count++;
        }
        return count;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Нормализует цикл — делает его независимым от точки старта и направления.
    /// </summary>
    private static string NormalizeCycle(List<Factor> cycle)
    {
        if (cycle.Count > 1 && cycle.First()?.Equals(cycle.Last()) == true)
            cycle.RemoveAt(cycle.Count - 1);

        var ordered = cycle
            .Select((v, i) => (v, i))
            .OrderBy(x => x.v?.Name)
            .First();

        var normalized = cycle.Skip(ordered.i).Concat(cycle.Take(ordered.i)).ToList();

        string forward = string.Join("→", normalized.Select(v => v.Name));
        string reverse = string.Join("→", normalized.Select(v => v.Name).Reverse());

        return string.Compare(forward, reverse, StringComparison.Ordinal) <= 0
            ? forward
            : reverse;
    }
}

CycleInfo.cs

using NKM1.Models;

namespace NKM1;

public class CycleInfo
{
    public List<Factor> Vertices { get; set; } = new();
    public bool IsPositive { get; set; }
    public double NegativeEdgeCount { get; set; }

    public override string ToString()
    {
        var sign = IsPositive ? "Положительный" : "Отрицательный ";
        return $"({sign}) [{string.Join("] -> [", Vertices.Select(v => v.Name))}]";
    }
}

ImpulseSimulator.cs

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using NKM1;       // NKM (graph)

namespace NKM1.Models
{
    public class SimulationResult
    {
        public List<string> VertexNames { get; set; } = new List<string>();
        public List<double[]> ValuesByStep { get; set; } = new List<double[]>();
    }

    public static class ImpulseSimulator
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Симуляция: graph, P0 (начальные импульсы по вершинам), steps.
        /// Все исходные v_исх принимаются равными 0.
        /// Возвращает SimulationResult для t = 0..steps.
        /// </summary>
        public static SimulationResult Simulate(NKM graph, IDictionary<Factor, double> P0, int steps)
        {
            if (graph == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(graph));
            if (steps < 0) throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(steps));

            var factors = graph.Vertices.ToList();
            int n = factors.Count;
            var indexOf = new Dictionary<Factor, int>();
            for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) indexOf[factors[i]] = i;

            double[] v_prev = new double[n];

            double[] v_curr = new double[n];
            if (P0 != null)
            {
                foreach (var kv in P0)
                {
                    if (indexOf.TryGetValue(kv.Key, out var idx)) v_curr[idx] = kv.Value;
                }
            }

            // Матрица весов W[j,i] (используем Link.Weight)
            double[,] W = new double[n, n];
            foreach (var e in graph.Edges)
            {
                var s = e.Source as Factor;
                var t = e.Target as Factor;
                if (s == null || t == null) continue;
                if (!indexOf.TryGetValue(s, out var js) || !indexOf.TryGetValue(t, out var ti)) continue;
                double w = Convert.ToDouble(e.Weight);
                W[js, ti] += w;
            }

            var result = new SimulationResult();
            result.VertexNames = factors.Select(f => f.Name).ToList();

            // Сохраняем t=0 (v_curr)
            result.ValuesByStep.Add((double[])v_curr.Clone());

            // Выполняем t = 0..steps-1 -> вычисляем v(t+1)
            for (int tstep = 0; tstep < steps; tstep++)
            {
                // p(t) = v_curr - v_prev
                double[] p = new double[n];
                for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) p[i] = v_curr[i] - v_prev[i];

                // delta_i = sum_j W[j,i] * p[j]
                double[] delta = new double[n];
                for (int j = 0; j < n; j++)
                {
                    if (p[j] == 0.0) continue;
                    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
                    {
                        var w = W[j, i];
                        if (w == 0.0) continue;
                        delta[i] += w * p[j];
                    }
                }

                // v_next = v_curr + delta
                double[] v_next = new double[n];
                for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) v_next[i] = v_curr[i] + delta[i];

                result.ValuesByStep.Add((double[])v_next.Clone());

                Array.Copy(v_curr, v_prev, n);
                Array.Copy(v_next, v_curr, n);
            }

            return result;
        }
    }
}

using GraphX.Common.Models;

/// <summary>
/// Ребро графа. В НКМ - связь между факторами с определённым весом.

public class Link : EdgeBase<Factor>
{

    {
        Weight = weight;
    }
    public override string ToString() => $"{Weight,8:F}";

MatrixAnalyzer.cs

using System.Numerics;
using MathNet.Numerics.LinearAlgebra;

namespace NKM1.Models;
/// <summary>
/// Класс для анализа графа через матрицу смежности.
/// </summary>
public static class GraphMatrixAnalyzer
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Преобразует граф в матрицу смежности с весами.
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="graph">Граф (например, NKM)</param>
    /// <returns>Матрица NxN, где N = количество вершин</returns>
    public static double[,] ToAdjacencyMatrix(NKM graph)
    {
        var vertices = graph.Vertices.ToList();
        int n = vertices.Count;
        var matrix = new double[n, n];

        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        {
            for (int j = 0; j < n; j++)
                matrix[i, j] = 0; // по умолчанию нет связи
        }

        foreach (var edge in graph.Edges)
        {
            int i = vertices.IndexOf(edge.Source);
            int j = vertices.IndexOf(edge.Target);
            matrix[i, j] = edge.Weight;
        }

        return matrix;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Вычисляет собственные числа матрицы смежности.
    /// </summary>
    public static Complex[] ComputeEigenvalues(double[,] adjacencyMatrix)
    {
        // Используем Math.NET Numerics
        var matrix = Matrix<double>.Build.DenseOfArray(adjacencyMatrix);
        var eigen = matrix.Evd();

        // Возвращаем все собственные значения
        return eigen.EigenValues.Select(c => new Complex(c.Real, c.Imaginary)).ToArray();
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Находит максимальное по модулю собственное число.
    /// </summary>
    public static Complex GetMaxEigenvalueByMagnitude(Complex[] eigenvalues)
    {
        return eigenvalues.OrderByDescending(e => e.Magnitude).FirstOrDefault();
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Быстрая связка: от графа до спектрального радиуса.
    /// </summary>
    public static double GetSpectralRadius(NKM graph)
    {
        var matrix = ToAdjacencyMatrix(graph);
        var eigenvalues = ComputeEigenvalues(matrix);
        return eigenvalues.Max(e => e.Magnitude);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Пример использования в коде.
    /// </summary>
    public static void ExampleUsage(NKM graph)
    {
        var matrix = ToAdjacencyMatrix(graph);
        var eigenvalues = ComputeEigenvalues(matrix);
        var maxEigen = GetMaxEigenvalueByMagnitude(eigenvalues);

        Console.WriteLine("Матрица смежности:");
        PrintMatrix(matrix);

        Console.WriteLine("\nСобственные числа:");
        foreach (var e in eigenvalues)
            Console.WriteLine($"λ = {e.Real:F3} {(e.Imaginary >= 0 ? "+" : "-")} {Math.Abs(e.Imaginary):F3}i");

        Console.WriteLine($"\nМаксимальное по модулю собственное число: |λmax| = {maxEigen.Magnitude:F3}");
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Утилита для красивого вывода матрицы в консоль.
    /// </summary>
    public static void PrintMatrix(double[,] matrix)
    {
        int n = matrix.GetLength(0);
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        {
            for (int j = 0; j < n; j++)
                Console.Write($"{matrix[i, j],8:F2}");
            Console.WriteLine();
        }
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// Простая структура комплексного числа, если Math.NET не подключен.
/// </summary>
// public struct Complex

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

NKM.cs

using QuickGraph;

namespace NKM1.Models
{
	/// <summary>
    /// Модель графа. Этот граф и является НКМ.
    /// </summary>
	public class NKM : BidirectionalGraph<Factor, Link>
    {
        private int _counter = 0;

        public NKM()
        {

        }

        public Factor AddVertex()
        {
            var v = new Factor("V" + (++_counter));
            base.AddVertex(v);
            return v;
        }

        public void RenameVertex(string oldId, string newId)
        {
            var v = Vertices.FirstOrDefault(x => x.Name == oldId);
            if (v != null) v.Name = newId;
        }


		public void RemoveVertex(string id)
		{
			RemoveVertexIf((v) => v.Name == id);
			RemoveEdgeIf((e) => e.Source?.Name == id || e.Target?.Name == id);
		}

		public bool AddEdge(Factor source, Factor target, double weight)
        {
            if (source is not null && target is not null) 
				return AddEdge(source.ID, target.ID, weight);
			else
				return false;
        }

        public bool AddEdge(long sourceId, long targetId, double weight)
        {
            var s = Vertices.FirstOrDefault(v => v.ID == sourceId);
            var t = Vertices.FirstOrDefault(v => v.ID == targetId);
            if (s != null && t != null && !EdgeExists(sourceId, targetId))
			{
                return base.AddEdge(new Link(s, t, weight));
            }
			else
			{
				return false;
			}
        }


        public void RemoveEdge(string sourceId, string targetId)
        {
            RemoveEdgeIf(e => e.Source?.Name == sourceId && e.Target?.Name == targetId);
        }


		public void SetEdgeWeight(string sourceId, string targetId, double w)
		{
			var e = Edges.FirstOrDefault(ed => ed.Source?.Name == sourceId && ed.Target?.Name == targetId);
			if (e != null) e.Weight = w;
		}
		
		public bool EdgeExists(Factor source, Factor target)
		=>	source is not null && target is not null
			&& EdgeExists(source.ID, target.ID);

		public bool EdgeExists(long sourceId, long targetId)
		=> Edges.Any(e => e.Source.ID == sourceId && e.Target.ID == targetId)
			|| Edges.Any(e => e.Source.ID == targetId && e.Target.ID == sourceId);

		public static NKM CreateRandomDirectedGraph(int vertexCount, int edgeCount, int? randomSeed = null)
		{
			if (vertexCount <= 0)
			{
				throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(vertexCount), "Количество вершин должно быть положительным.");
			}

			// Максимальное количество ребер в простом ориентированном графе
			var maxEdges = vertexCount * (vertexCount - 1);
			if (edgeCount < 0 || edgeCount > maxEdges)
			{
				throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(edgeCount), $"Количество ребер должно быть в диапазоне от 0 до {maxEdges}.");
			}

			var graph = new NKM();
			var random = randomSeed.HasValue ? new Random(randomSeed.Value) : new Random();

			// 1. Создаем вершины и сохраняем их в массив для быстрого доступа
			var vertices = new Factor[vertexCount];
			for (int i = 0; i < vertexCount; i++)
			{
				vertices[i] = graph.AddVertex();
			}

			// 2. Создаем и добавляем случайные ребра
			var existingEdges = new HashSet<Tuple<int, int>>();
			while (graph.EdgeCount < edgeCount)
			{
				// Выбираем случайную исходную и целевую вершины
				var sourceIndex = random.Next(0, vertexCount);
				var targetIndex = random.Next(0, vertexCount);

				// Проверяем, чтобы не было самопетель и дублирующихся ребер
				if (sourceIndex == targetIndex)
				{
					continue;
				}

				var newEdgeTuple = new Tuple<int, int>(sourceIndex, targetIndex);
				if (!existingEdges.Contains(newEdgeTuple))
				{
					var sourceVertex = vertices[sourceIndex];
					var targetVertex = vertices[targetIndex];
					// Создаем ребро со случайным весом
					var weight = (random.Next(0, 2) == 0 ? 1 : -1) * random.NextDouble();
					graph.AddEdge(sourceVertex.ID, targetVertex.ID, weight);

					existingEdges.Add(newEdgeTuple);
				}
			}

			return graph;
		}
	}


}

GraphFileService.cs

using NKM1.DTO;
using NKM1.Models;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Globalization;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Text.Json;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using System.Windows.Controls;

namespace NKM1.Service
{
    public static class GraphFileService
    {
        public static void Save(NKM graph, GraphX.Controls.GraphArea<Factor, Link, NKM> graphArea, string path)
        {
            var dto = new GraphFileDto();
            dto.X0 = 0; dto.Y0 = 0;

            // Вершины
            foreach (var v in graph.Vertices)
            {
                double x = 0, y = 0;
                if (graphArea.VertexList.TryGetValue(v, out var vc))
                {
                    x = Canvas.GetLeft(vc);
                    y = Canvas.GetTop(vc);
                }

                dto.Vertices.Add(new VertexDto
                {
                    Name = v.Name,
                    X = x,
                    Y = y,
                    Radius = 20,
                    Background = "#ffffff",
                    FontSize = 18,
                    Color = "#000000",
                    Border = "#000000"
                });
            }

            // Рёбра
            foreach (var e in graph.Edges)
            {
                int idx1 = graph.Vertices.ToList().IndexOf(e.Source);
                int idx2 = graph.Vertices.ToList().IndexOf(e.Target);
                dto.Edges.Add(new EdgeDto
                {
                    Vertex1 = idx1,
                    Vertex2 = idx2,
                    Weight = e.Weight.ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
                    IsDirected = true,
                    ControlStep = 0,
                    FontSize = 18,
                    LineWidth = 2,
                    Background = "#000000",
                    Color = "#000000"
                });
            }

            dto.Texts = new List<object>();

            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(dto, new JsonSerializerOptions { WriteIndented = true });
            File.WriteAllText(path, json, Encoding.UTF8);
        }

        public static void Load(NKM graph, GraphX.Controls.GraphArea<Factor, Link, NKM> graphArea, string path)
        {
            var json = File.ReadAllText(path, Encoding.UTF8);
            var dto = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<GraphFileDto>(json);
            if (dto == null) throw new Exception("Не удалось распарсить файл");

            foreach (var e in graph.Vertices)
            {
                graph.RemoveVertex(e);
            }

            // создаём вершины
            foreach (var vdto in dto.Vertices)
                graph.AddVertex(new Factor(vdto.Name));

            // создаём рёбра
            foreach (var edto in dto.Edges)
            {
                var s = graph.Vertices.ElementAt(edto.Vertex1);
                var t = graph.Vertices.ElementAt(edto.Vertex2);
                if (double.TryParse(edto.Weight, NumberStyles.Any, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out double w))
                    graph.AddEdge(s, t, w);
            }

            // обновляем визуал
            graphArea.GenerateGraph(true, true);

            // расставляем позиции
            //for (int i = 0; i < dto.Vertices.Count; i++)
            //{
            //    if (graphArea.VertexList.TryGetValue(graph.Vertices.ElementAt(i), out var vc))
            //    {
            //        Canvas.SetLeft(vc, dto.Vertices[i].X);
            //        Canvas.SetTop(vc, dto.Vertices[i].Y);
            //    }
            //}
        }
    }
}

AddEdgeWindow.xaml.cs

using NKM1.Models;
using System;
using System.Linq;
using System.Windows;

namespace NKM1.Visual;

public partial class AddEdgeWindow : Window
{
    private readonly NKM graph;
    public Factor Source { get; private set; }
    public Factor Target { get; private set; }
    public double Weight { get; private set; }

    public AddEdgeWindow(NKM graph)
    {
        InitializeComponent();
        this.graph = graph;

        // Заполняем списки факторами
        var names = graph.Vertices.Select(v => v.Name).ToList();
        CmbSource.ItemsSource = names;
        CmbTarget.ItemsSource = names;
    }

    private void CmbSource_SelectionChanged(object sender, System.Windows.Controls.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
    {
        if (CmbSource.SelectedItem == null) return;
        string selected = CmbSource.SelectedItem.ToString();
        CmbTarget.ItemsSource = graph.Vertices
            .Select(v => v.Name)
            .Where(name => name != selected)
            .ToList();
    }

    private void CmbTarget_SelectionChanged(object sender, System.Windows.Controls.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
    {
        if (CmbTarget.SelectedItem == null) return;
        string selected = CmbTarget.SelectedItem.ToString();
        CmbSource.ItemsSource = graph.Vertices
            .Select(v => v.Name)
            .Where(name => name != selected)
            .ToList();
    }

    private void BtnAdd_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
    {
        if (CmbSource.SelectedItem == null || CmbTarget.SelectedItem == null)
        {
            MessageBox.Show("Выберите источник и цель.", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Warning);
            return;
        }

        if (!double.TryParse(TxtWeight.Text.Replace(',', '.'), System.Globalization.NumberStyles.Float, System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out double weight))
        {
            MessageBox.Show("Введите корректное число.", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Warning);
            return;
        }

        if (weight < -1 || weight > 1)
        {
            MessageBox.Show("Значение оценки связи должно быть в диапазоне [-1; 1].", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Warning);
            return;
        }

        if (weight == 0)
        {
            MessageBox.Show("Значение оценки связи должно быть отлично от 0", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Warning);
            return;
        }


        var sourceName = CmbSource.SelectedItem.ToString();
        var targetName = CmbTarget.SelectedItem.ToString();
        var source = graph.Vertices.First(e => e.Name == sourceName );
        var target = graph.Vertices.First(e => e.Name == targetName);

        if (graph.EdgeExists(source, target))
        {
            MessageBox.Show($"Связь между факторами '{sourceName}' и '{targetName}' ужа существует.", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Warning);
            return;
        }

        Source = source;
        Target = target;
        Weight = weight;

        DialogResult = true;
    }

    private void BtnCancel_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
    {
        DialogResult = false;
    }
}

using NKM1.Models;
using System;

using System.Windows.Media.Imaging;
using System.Windows.Shapes;
using System.Xml.Linq;

namespace NKM1.Visual
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Interaction logic for AddVertexWindow.xaml
    /// </summary>
    public partial class AddVertexWindow : Window
    {
        public string Name { get; set; }
        private NKM graph;

        public AddVertexWindow(NKM graph)
        {
            this.graph = graph;
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private void BtnAdd_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var name = TxtName.Text.Trim();

            // Проверка заполнения
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(name))
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Введите имя фактора.", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Warning);
                return;
            }

            // Проверка уникальности
            if (graph.Vertices.Any(v => v.Name.Equals(name, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Фактор с таким именем уже существует.", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Error);
                return;
            }

            Name = name;
            DialogResult = true;
        }

        private void BtnCancel_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            DialogResult = false;
        }
    }
}

DataGraphLogicCore.cs

using GraphX.Common.Enums;
using GraphX.Logic.Algorithms.LayoutAlgorithms;
using GraphX.Logic.Models;
using NKM1.Models;

namespace NKM1.Visual;

public class DataGraphLogicCore : GXLogicCore<Factor, Link, NKM>
{
    public DataGraphLogicCore()
    {
        SetProperties();
    }

    public DataGraphLogicCore(NKM graph) : base(graph)
    {
        Graph = graph;
        SetProperties();
    }

    private void SetProperties()
    {
        DefaultLayoutAlgorithm = LayoutAlgorithmTypeEnum.KK;
        DefaultOverlapRemovalAlgorithm = OverlapRemovalAlgorithmTypeEnum.FSA;
        DefaultEdgeRoutingAlgorithm = EdgeRoutingAlgorithmTypeEnum.SimpleER;
        AsyncAlgorithmCompute = false;
    }
}

EditEdgeWindow.xaml.cs

using NKM1.Models;
using System;
using System.Linq;
using System.Windows;

namespace NKM1.Visual;

public partial class EditEdgeWindow : Window
{
    private readonly NKM graph;
    public Factor Source { get; private set; }
    public Factor Target { get; private set; }
    public double Weight { get; private set; }

    public EditEdgeWindow(NKM graph, Link link)
    {
        this.graph = graph;
        this.Source = link.Source;
        this.Target = link.Target;
        this.Weight = link.Weight;
        InitializeComponent();

        TxtWeight.Text = Weight.ToString();

        string selected = link.Target.Name; 
        CmbSource.ItemsSource = graph.Vertices
            .Select(v => v.Name)
            .Where(name => name != selected)
            .ToList();

        selected = link.Source.Name;
        CmbTarget.ItemsSource = graph.Vertices
            .Select(v => v.Name)
            .Where(name => name != selected)
            .ToList();

        CmbSource.Text = link.Source.Name;
        CmbSource.SelectedItem = link.Source.Name;
        CmbTarget.Text = link.Target.Name;
        CmbTarget.SelectedItem = link.Target.Name;
    }

    private void CmbSource_SelectionChanged(object sender, System.Windows.Controls.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
    {
        if (CmbSource.SelectedItem == null) return;
        string selected = CmbSource.SelectedItem.ToString();
        CmbTarget.ItemsSource = graph.Vertices
            .Select(v => v.Name)
            .Where(name => name != selected)
            .ToList();
    }

    private void CmbTarget_SelectionChanged(object sender, System.Windows.Controls.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
    {
        if (CmbTarget.SelectedItem == null) return;
        string selected = CmbTarget.SelectedItem.ToString();
        CmbSource.ItemsSource = graph.Vertices
            .Select(v => v.Name)
            .Where(name => name != selected)
            .ToList();
    }

    private void BtnAdd_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)

        if (CmbSource.SelectedItem == null || CmbTarget.SelectedItem == null)

            return;

        {
            MessageBox.Show("Значение должно быть в диапазоне [-1; 1].", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Warning);
            return;

        if (weight == 0)
        {
            MessageBox.Show("Значение оценки связи должно быть отлично от 0", "Ошибка", MessageBoxButton.OK, MessageBoxImage.Warning);
            return;

        var targetName = CmbTarget.SelectedItem.ToString();

StructureAnalizys.xaml.cs

using NKM1.Models;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using System.Windows;
using System.Windows.Controls;
using System.Windows.Data;
using System.Windows.Documents;
using System.Windows.Input;
using System.Windows.Media;
using System.Windows.Media.Imaging;
using System.Windows.Shapes;

namespace NKM1.Visual;

/// <summary>
/// Interaction logic for StructureAnalizys.xaml
/// </summary>
public partial class StructureAnalizys : Window
{
    private NKM nkm;

    public StructureAnalizys(NKM nkm)
    {
        this.nkm = nkm;
        InitializeComponent();
        Run();
    }

    private void Run()
    {
        {
            var builder = new StringBuilder();
            var factors = nkm.Vertices.Count();
            var links = nkm.Edges.Count();
            var cycles = CycleDetection.FindAllSimpleCycles(nkm).OrderBy(c => c.IsPositive).ToList();
            var matrix = GraphMatrixAnalyzer.ToAdjacencyMatrix(nkm);
            var eigenvalues = GraphMatrixAnalyzer.ComputeEigenvalues(matrix);
            var maxEigen = GraphMatrixAnalyzer.GetMaxEigenvalueByMagnitude(eigenvalues);

            builder.AppendLine("[АНАЛИЗ СТРУКТУРНОЙ УСТРОЙЧИВОСТИ]");
            builder.AppendLine("----------------------------------");
            builder.AppendLine();

            builder.AppendLine($"Факторов: {factors}");
            builder.AppendLine($"Связей: {links}");
            builder.AppendLine();

            builder.AppendLine($"Циклов: {cycles.Count()}");
            builder.AppendLine($"Положительных циклов: {cycles.Count(c => c.IsPositive)}");
            builder.AppendLine($"Отрицательных циклов: {cycles.Count(c => !c.IsPositive)}");
            builder.AppendLine();
            for (int i = 0; i < cycles.Count; i++)
            {
                builder.AppendLine($"Цикл {i}: {cycles[i].ToString()} ");
            }
            builder.AppendLine();
            builder.AppendLine("ВЫВОД: ");
            builder.AppendLine(cycles.Count(c => !c.IsPositive) % 2 == 0 ? "НКМ структурно не устойчива" : "НКМ структурно устойчива");
            builder.AppendLine();

            builder.AppendLine("[АНАЛИЗ УСТОЙЧИВОСТИ ПО ВОЗМУЩЕНИЮ, ПО НАЧАЛЬНОМУ ЗНАЧЕНИЮ]");
            builder.AppendLine("-----------------------------------------------------------");

            builder.AppendLine("Собственные числа:");
            int j = 0;
            foreach (var e in eigenvalues)
            {
                builder.Append($"λ_{++j} = {e.Real:F3} ");
                if (e.Imaginary != 0)
                    builder.Append($"{(e.Imaginary >= 0 ? "+" : "-")} {Math.Abs(e.Imaginary):F3}i");
                builder.AppendLine();
            }

            builder.AppendLine();

            builder.AppendLine($"Максимальное по модулю собственное число: |λmax| = {maxEigen.Magnitude:F3}");
            builder.AppendLine();

            builder.AppendLine("ВЫВОД: ");
            builder.AppendLine(maxEigen.Magnitude < 1 ? "НКМ устойчива по возмущению, по начальному значению." : "НКМ не устойчива по возмущению, по начальному значению");
            builder.AppendLine();
            Result.Text = builder.ToString();
        }
    }
}
